UNITY_LOCATION(6) uniform mediump sampler2D _ClothTex;
in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
in highp vec4 in_TANGENT0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
out highp vec3 vs_TEXCOORD2;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD7;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
vec4 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
vec4 u_xlat2;
vec4 u_xlat3;
vec3 u_xlat4;
vec3 u_xlat5;
float u_xlat15;
void main()
{
    u_xlat0.x = fract(_Time.x);
    u_xlat0.xy = u_xlat0.xx * _DigiST1.zw;
    u_xlat0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _DigiST1.xy + u_xlat0.xy;
    u_xlat0.x = textureLod(_ClothTex, u_xlat0.xy, 0.0).z;
    u_xlat5.xyz = in_NORMAL0.xyz * vec3(_DigiDistore);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * vec3(0.200000003, 0.200000003, 0.200000003) + in_POSITION0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyw = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * u_xlat0.xxx + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * u_xlat0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = u_xlat1.xy * vec2(vec2(_FurTilling, _FurTilling));
    gl_Position = u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyw = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat2.w = u_xlat1.x;
    u_xlat3.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat3.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat3.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat2;
    u_xlat3.w = u_xlat1.y;
    u_xlat4.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat4.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat3;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat2.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat2.yzx * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD7 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD8 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    return;
}

void main()
{
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = texture(_FurTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_1 = u_xlat16_0.x * 2.0 + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_1 = u_xlat16_1 * _FurShape;
    u_xlat16_1 = u_xlat16_1 * u_xlat16_0.y + 1.0;
    u_xlat17.xz = vec2(u_xlat16_1) * vs_TEXCOORD0.xy;
    u_xlat1 = texture(_MainTex, u_xlat17.xz);
    u_xlat16_2 = texture(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_3.x = log2(abs(u_xlat16_2.z));
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * _AOScale;
    u_xlat16_3.x = exp2(u_xlat16_3.x);
    u_xlat16_20 = u_xlat16_2.x + _MetallicOffset;
    u_xlat16_37 = u_xlat16_2.y + _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat16_3.z = max(u_xlat16_37, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_3.xz = min(u_xlat16_3.xz, vec2(1.0, 1.0));
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = texture(_BumpMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_4.xy = u_xlat16_4.xy * vec2(vec2(_NormalScale, _NormalScale));
    u_xlat16_54 = u_xlat16_2.w * _EmisssionScale;
    u_xlat16_54 = u_xlat16_54 * _Emissive;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_4.yyy * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyw = u_xlat16_4.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz + u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_4.zzz * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyw;
    u_xlat16_55 = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat16_55 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_55);
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_55) * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_5.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_5.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat17.x = dot(u_xlat16_5.xyz, u_xlat16_5.xyz);
    u_xlat17.x = max(u_xlat17.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat17.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat17.x);
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat17.xxx * u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat6.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat7.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset0.xyz;
    vec3 txVec0 = vec3(u_xlat7.xy,u_xlat7.z);
    u_xlat7.x = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec0, 0.0);
    u_xlat8.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset1.xyz;
    vec3 txVec1 = vec3(u_xlat8.xy,u_xlat8.z);
    u_xlat7.y = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec1, 0.0);
    u_xlat8.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset2.xyz;
    vec3 txVec2 = vec3(u_xlat8.xy,u_xlat8.z);
    u_xlat7.z = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec2, 0.0);
    u_xlat8.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset3.xyz;
    vec3 txVec3 = vec3(u_xlat8.xy,u_xlat8.z);
    u_xlat7.w = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec3, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_55 = dot(u_xlat7, vec4(0.25, 0.25, 0.25, 0.25));
    u_xlat16_56 = (-_MainLightShadowParams.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_55 = u_xlat16_55 * _MainLightShadowParams.x + u_xlat16_56;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb51 = !!(0.0>=vs_TEXCOORD7.z);
#else
    u_xlatb51 = 0.0>=vs_TEXCOORD7.z;
#endif
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb53 = !!(vs_TEXCOORD7.z>=1.0);
#else
    u_xlatb53 = vs_TEXCOORD7.z>=1.0;
#endif
    u_xlatb51 = u_xlatb51 || u_xlatb53;
    u_xlat16_55 = (u_xlatb51) ? 1.0 : u_xlat16_55;
    u_xlat16_56 = (-u_xlat16_20) * 0.959999979 + 0.959999979;
    u_xlat16_56 = (-u_xlat16_56) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_20 = u_xlat16_20;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_20 = min(max(u_xlat16_20, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_20 = clamp(u_xlat16_20, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = (-u_xlat1.xyz) * vec3(u_xlat16_20) + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat7.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz + vec3(-0.0399999991, -0.0399999991, -0.0399999991);
    u_xlat7.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_20) * u_xlat7.xyz + vec3(0.0399999991, 0.0399999991, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_20 = (-u_xlat16_3.z) + u_xlat16_56;
    u_xlat16_20 = u_xlat16_20 + 1.0;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_20 = min(max(u_xlat16_20, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_20 = clamp(u_xlat16_20, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_56 = u_xlat16_3.z * u_xlat16_3.z;
    u_xlat51 = u_xlat16_56 * u_xlat16_56;
    u_xlat8.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * u_xlat17.xxx + _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    u_xlat17.x = dot(u_xlat8.xyz, u_xlat8.xyz);
    u_xlat17.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat17.x);
    u_xlat8.xyz = u_xlat17.xxx * u_xlat8.xyz;
    u_xlat17.x = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
    u_xlat53 = u_xlat17.x;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat53 = min(max(u_xlat53, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat53 = clamp(u_xlat53, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_5.x = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_5.x = abs(u_xlat16_5.x) + 0.00400000019;
    u_xlat16_5.x = min(u_xlat16_5.x, 1.0);
    u_xlat57 = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat8.xyz);
    u_xlat58 = u_xlat57;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat58 = min(max(u_xlat58, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat58 = clamp(u_xlat58, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat59 = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat8.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat59 = min(max(u_xlat59, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat59 = clamp(u_xlat59, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat10.x = u_xlat16_4.y * u_xlat16_4.y;
    u_xlat27 = u_xlat16_4.y * 0.25;
    u_xlat10.z = u_xlat10.x * 0.125 + u_xlat27;
    u_xlat10.x = u_xlat10.x * 0.125 + (-u_xlat27);
    u_xlat11.xy = u_xlat10.zx + vec2(0.125, 0.125);
    u_xlat16_22.xy = max(u_xlat11.xy, vec2(0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_22.xy = u_xlat16_22.xy * vec2(vec2(_SHScale, _SHScale));
    u_xlat16_12.xyz = u_xlat16_22.yyy * _SHBotColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_12.xyz = u_xlat16_22.xxx * _SHTopColor.xyz + u_xlat16_12.xyz;
    u_xlat16_12.xyz = u_xlat16_12.xyz * _SHColorScale.xyz;
    u_xlat16_22.x = dot((-u_xlat2.xyz), u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat16_22.x = u_xlat16_22.x + u_xlat16_22.x;
    u_xlat16_13.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * (-u_xlat16_22.xxx) + (-u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = (-u_xlat16_5.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_22.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat16_22.x = u_xlat16_22.x * u_xlat16_22.x;
    u_xlat16_12.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xxx * u_xlat16_12.xyz;
    u_xlat16_39 = (-u_xlat16_3.z) * 0.699999988 + 1.70000005;
    u_xlat16_39 = u_xlat16_3.z * u_xlat16_39;
    u_xlat16_39 = u_xlat16_39 * 6.0;
    u_xlat16_10 = textureLod(unity_SpecCube0, u_xlat16_13.xyz, u_xlat16_39);
    u_xlat16_39 = u_xlat16_10.w + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_39 = unity_SpecCube0_HDR.w * u_xlat16_39 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_39 = max(u_xlat16_39, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_39 = log2(u_xlat16_39);
    u_xlat16_39 = u_xlat16_39 * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.y;
    u_xlat16_39 = exp2(u_xlat16_39);
    u_xlat16_39 = u_xlat16_39 * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.x;
    u_xlat16_13.xyz = u_xlat16_10.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_39);
    u_xlat16_13.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xxx * u_xlat16_13.xyz;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat16_56 * u_xlat16_56 + 1.0;
    u_xlat2.x = float(1.0) / u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat16_13.xyz * u_xlat2.xxx;
    u_xlat10.xyz = (-u_xlat7.xyz) + vec3(u_xlat16_20);
    u_xlat10.xyz = u_xlat16_22.xxx * u_xlat10.xyz + u_xlat7.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat2.xyz * u_xlat10.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat16_12.xyz * u_xlat16_9.xyz + u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat10.x = u_xlat17.x * 0.5 + 0.5;
    u_xlat10.y = 0.5;
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = texture(_RampTex, u_xlat10.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_12.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_55) * u_xlat6.xyz;
    u_xlat16_12.xyz = u_xlat16_12.xyz * _MainLightColor.www;
    u_xlat16_20 = (-_RampSmooth) * 0.5 + _RampThreshold;
    u_xlat16_22.x = _RampSmooth * 0.5 + _RampThreshold;

    u_xlat6.x = u_xlat53 * u_xlat16_55 + (-u_xlat16_20);
    u_xlat17.x = float(1.0) / u_xlat17.x;
    u_xlat17.x = u_xlat17.x * u_xlat6.x;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat17.x = min(max(u_xlat17.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat17.x = clamp(u_xlat17.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat6.x = u_xlat17.x * -2.0 + 3.0;
    u_xlat17.x = u_xlat17.x * u_xlat17.x;
    u_xlat16_20 = dot(u_xlat6.xx, u_xlat17.xx);
    u_xlat16_20 = u_xlat16_20 + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_20 = u_xlat16_0.x + u_xlat16_20;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_20 = min(max(u_xlat16_20, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_20 = clamp(u_xlat16_20, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_13.xyz = (-_SketchColor.xyz) + vec3(1.0, 1.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_13.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_20) * u_xlat16_13.xyz + _SketchColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_12.xyz = u_xlat16_12.xyz * u_xlat16_13.xyz;
    u_xlat11.xy = u_xlat16_3.zz * vec2(_glossiness_1X, _glossiness_1Y);
    u_xlat11.zw = u_xlat16_3.zz * vec2(_glossiness_2X, _glossiness_2Y);
    u_xlat17.x = u_xlat16_0.x * _SunShift;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat16_0.x * _SunShift + _SunShiftOffuse1;
    u_xlat16_13.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz * u_xlat0.xxx + vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_20 = dot(u_xlat16_13.xyz, u_xlat16_13.xyz);
    u_xlat16_20 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_20);
    u_xlat16_13.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_20) * u_xlat16_13.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat17.x * 0.5 + _SunShiftOffuse2;
    u_xlat16_14.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz * u_xlat0.xxx + vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_20 = dot(u_xlat16_14.xyz, u_xlat16_14.xyz);
    u_xlat16_20 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_20);
    u_xlat16_14.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_20) * u_xlat16_14.xyz;
    u_xlat16_15.xyz = u_xlat16_9.xyz * _specularColor1.xyz;
    u_xlat16 = u_xlat11.xyyw * u_xlat11.xyxz;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat8.xyz, u_xlat16_13.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat0.x;

float u_xlat15;
void main()
{
    u_xlat0.x = fract(_Time.x);
    u_xlat0.xy = u_xlat0.xx * _DigiST1.zw;
    u_xlat0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _DigiST1.xy + u_xlat0.xy;
    u_xlat0.x = textureLod(_ClothTex, u_xlat0.xy, 0.0).z;
    u_xlat5.xyz = in_NORMAL0.xyz * vec3(_DigiDistore);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * vec3(0.200000003, 0.200000003, 0.200000003) + in_POSITION0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyw = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * u_xlat0.xxx + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * u_xlat0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = u_xlat1.xy * vec2(vec2(_FurTilling, _FurTilling));
    gl_Position = u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1.xyw = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat2.w = u_xlat1.x;
    u_xlat3.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat3.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat3.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat2;
    u_xlat3.w = u_xlat1.y;
    u_xlat4.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat4.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat3;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat2.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat2.yzx * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD7 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD8 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    return;
}

    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_2.x + (-_DigiBaseColor0.w);
    u_xlat16_16.x = max(_DigiChange, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_16.x = min(u_xlat16_16.x, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_16.x * u_xlat16_2.x + _DigiBaseColor0.w;
    u_xlat14.x = fract(_Time.x);
    u_xlat7.xy = u_xlat14.xx * _DigiST1.zw;
    u_xlat7.xy = vs_TEXCOORD0.xy * _DigiST1.xy + u_xlat7.xy;
    u_xlat10_14 = texture2D(_ClothTex, u_xlat7.xy).x;
    u_xlat14.x = u_xlat10_14 + vs_TEXCOORD0.y;
    u_xlat14.x = (-u_xlat16_2.x) + u_xlat14.x;
    u_xlat14.x = clamp(u_xlat14.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat9.xyz = u_xlat14.xxx * u_xlat0.xzw + u_xlat1.xyz;
    SV_Target0 = u_xlat9;
    return;
}

#endif
"
}

UNITY_LOCATION(6) uniform mediump sampler2D _ClothTex;
in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
in highp vec4 in_TANGENT0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;

out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;

void main()
{
    u_xlat0.x = fract(_Time.x);
    u_xlat0.xy = u_xlat0.xx * _DigiST1.zw;
    u_xlat0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _DigiST1.xy + u_xlat0.xy;
    u_xlat0.x = textureLod(_ClothTex, u_xlat0.xy, 0.0).z;
    u_xlat5.xyz = in_NORMAL0.xyz * vec3(_DigiDistore);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * vec3(0.200000003, 0.200000003, 0.200000003) + in_POSITION0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyw = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * u_xlat0.xxx + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * u_xlat0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = u_xlat1.xy * vec2(vec2(_FurTilling, _FurTilling));
    gl_Position = u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1.xyw = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat2.w = u_xlat1.x;
    u_xlat3.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat3.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat3.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat2;
    u_xlat3.w = u_xlat1.y;
    u_xlat4.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat4.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat3;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat2.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat2.yzx * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD7 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD8 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    return;
}

mediump float u_xlat16_32;
mediump float u_xlat16_35;
mediump float u_xlat16_42;
float u_xlat43;
float u_xlat44;
float u_xlat45;
mediump float u_xlat16_49;
mediump float u_xlat16_50;
mediump float u_xlat16_53;
void main()
{
    u_xlat16_0.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_0.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_0.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(u_xlat16_0.xyz, u_xlat16_0.xyz);
    u_xlat1.x = max(u_xlat1.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat1.x);
    u_xlat15.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * u_xlat1.xxx + _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * u_xlat1.xxx;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(u_xlat15.xyz, u_xlat15.xyz);
    u_xlat1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat1.x);
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.xxx * u_xlat15.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = texture(_FurTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat43 = u_xlat16_3.x * _SunShift;
    u_xlat43 = u_xlat43 * 0.5 + _SunShiftOffuse2;
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz * vec3(u_xlat43) + vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_42 = dot(u_xlat16_0.xyz, u_xlat16_0.xyz);
    u_xlat16_42 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_42);
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_42) * u_xlat16_0.xyz;
    u_xlat43 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat16_0.xyz);
    u_xlat43 = u_xlat43 * u_xlat43;
    u_xlat16_0 = texture(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_0.y + _RoughNessOffset;

    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyw * vec3(0.200000003, 0.200000003, 0.200000003) + u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyw = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * u_xlat0.xxx + u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * u_xlat0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat3.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat3.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat3.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat12 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat12 = max(u_xlat12, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat12 = inversesqrt(u_xlat12);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat12) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat1.w = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat1.w = min(max(u_xlat1.w, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat1.w = clamp(u_xlat1.w, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat1.xyz = in_COLOR0.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat12 = in_TEXCOORD0.y * 2.0 + 3.0;
    u_xlat1.z = (-_DigiChange) * 2.0 + u_xlat12;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat1.z = min(max(u_xlat1.z, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat1.z = clamp(u_xlat1.z, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat1.xyw = in_TEXCOORD0.xyy;
    vs_TEXCOORD2 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    gl_Position = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    return;
}

#endif
#ifdef FRAGMENT
#version 300 es

precision highp float;
precision highp int;
#define HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS 1
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
#define UNITY_UNIFORM
#else
#define UNITY_UNIFORM uniform
#endif

#if UNITY_SUPPORTS_UNIFORM_LOCATION

#define UNITY_BINDING(x) layout(binding = x, std140)
#else

#define UNITY_BINDING(x) layout(std140)
#endif
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS

#endif
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _OutlineColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _OutlineWidth;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _Offset;
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 _lightDir;
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 _ScreenResolution;
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 _DigiST1;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _DigiChange;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _DigiBaseColor0;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _DigiBaseColor1;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _DigiHighColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM float _DigiScale;
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
};
#endif
UNITY_LOCATION(0) uniform mediump sampler2D _ClothTex;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD2;
layout(location = 0) out mediump vec4 SV_Target0;
float u_xlat0;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_1;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_2;
mediump vec2 u_xlat16_3;
bool u_xlatb9;
mediump float u_xlat16_10;
void main()
{
    u_xlat0 = vs_TEXCOORD1.w * vs_TEXCOORD2.w;
    u_xlat16_1.x = _DigiChange;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_1.x = min(max(u_xlat16_1.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_1.x = clamp(u_xlat16_1.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_2 = (-_DigiBaseColor0) + _DigiBaseColor1;
    u_xlat16_1 = u_xlat16_1.xxxx * u_xlat16_2 + _DigiBaseColor0;
    u_xlat16_3.xy = texture(_ClothTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xy;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb9 = !!(u_xlat16_1.w>=u_xlat16_3.x);
#else
    u_xlatb9 = u_xlat16_1.w>=u_xlat16_3.x;
#endif
    u_xlat16_10 = (u_xlatb9) ? u_xlat0 : 0.0;
    u_xlat16_10 = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_10;
    u_xlat16_2.x = _DigiChange + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_2.x = (-u_xlat16_2.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_3.y * u_xlat16_2.x;
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_2.x * vs_TEXCOORD2.z;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xxx * _DigiHighColor.xyz;
    SV_Target0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_10) * u_xlat16_1.xyz + u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    SV_Target0.w = 1.0;
    return;
}

#endif
"
}
